  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_23ea09cb-2350-48e0-9880-ab504ccaa599'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText3008297686763179557" style="display:none">He was my boss, my brother’s friend, a Widower, an ex-felon, and a man I’d seen casually with a handful of women. But he was everything that gripped me, both the good and the bad. Worst case scenario if things turned awkward between us, I could go somewhere else. I’d gotten over epic heartbreak before, one more wouldn’t kill me. <br /><br />After moving to Austin following six months of unemployment back home, Iris Taylor knows she should be glad to have landed a job so quickly... even if the business is owned by a member of the same motorcycle club her estranged father used to belong to. Except Dex Locke might just be the biggest jerk she’s ever met. He’s rude, impatient and doesn’t know how to tell time. <br /><br />And the last thing they ever expected was each other. <br /><br />But it was either the strip club or the tattoo shop. <br /><br />… she should have chosen the strip club.</span>

<div id="review_877287798" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/877287798" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/877287798?book_show_action=true">Nov 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/29884738-under-locke">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=bikers">bikers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=pregnant-heroines">pregnant-heroines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer877287798" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18265416735800321350">Please see more of my reviews at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.bookaddicthaven.com'>www.bookaddicthaven.com</a><br/><br/>Although this was not the raunchy, offensive, biker romance that I had anticipated, I really liked 'Under Locke'. Unlike most MC romances, this story does not focus heavily around the debauchery of the clubhouse and the biker lifestyle. There is a little danger and some club business, but it is more in the background vs. being the central focus of the story.<br/><br/>'Under Locke' is a very slow-burn romance. It did take some time for me to get into </span>
  <span id="freeText18265416735800321350" style="display:none">Please see more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a><br /><br />Although this was not the raunchy, offensive, biker romance that I had anticipated, I really liked 'Under Locke'. Unlike most MC romances, this story does not focus heavily around the debauchery of the clubhouse and the biker lifestyle. There is a little danger and some club business, but it is more in the background vs. being the central focus of the story.<br /><br />'Under Locke' is a very slow-burn romance. It did take some time for me to get into this story. However, once I did, I was hooked. This author definitely didn't rush anything. I thought I would combust long before these two even kissed. There was plenty of anticipation and sexual frustration with this one!<br /><br />Iris Taylor, aka "Ritz", has recently moved to Austin. Iris is broke and looking for a fresh start, after death and disease have upended her life. She is staying with her half-brother, Sonny, who has hooked her up with a job at a tattoo shop owned by his friend, Dex.<br /><br />In no time, Iris figures out why Dex is in need of help. The guy is a royal a$$hole! He has managed to chase off a string of assistants before Ritz with his rude, insulting behavior. Dex has a total lack of patience and a hot temper. He says what he's thinking before stopping to think about how nasty or inappropriate his comments might be. Yeah, it took me a while to warm up to this guy.<br /><br />Iris is the polar opposite of Dex. She's sweet and innocent, having missed out on a lot of life's experiences as she was forced at a young age to become the sole provider for her younger brother after her mother fell ill. After her mother's health issues, Iris was faced with her own health crisis and then the death of her grandmother. Needless to say, her life was not easy and it didn't allow a lot of time for the usual parties and dating that comprised the social life of most young women her age.<br /><br />That being said, this book does have one of the big romance genre clichés that will drive some readers crazy. Iris is the quintessential naïve, good girl virgin. Dex is anything but virgin-like. He's the stereotypical manwhore that has slept around with a large part of Austin's female population without discrimination. This isn't really a problem for me, but I thought I'd mention it because I know it is something that many readers can't stand. <br /><br />Despite their differences, Iris and Dex find themselves attracted to each other. Dex tries to stay away from Ritz out of loyalty to her brother. She tries to deny her attraction to him because she knows that he is nothing but trouble. <br /><br />What follows is a series of absurdly jealous actions by Dex, while a clueless Iris wonders why he is acting like such a jerk. Perhaps if I was in a different mood when I listened to this story, I might have been irritated. As it is, I found their back and fort antics to be highly amusing.<br /><br />One thing that the two of them have in common is deadbeat fathers. When Ritz's sperm donor messes with some dangerous people, Sonny and her are placed in danger. This led to some interesting situations and a mild sense of suspense. However, I can't say that I ever had that "on the edge of my seat" anxious feeling.<br /><br />In the end, things work themselves out. There was plenty of back and forth throughout the book, followed by plenty of groveling. That was a big plus for me. I love it when my heroes have to do some groveling! <br /><br />Overall, it was a nice, sweet story. It was different from other MC romances that I've read, but that was okay. This was my first book by this author, but definitely won't be my last.<br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="18265416735800321350" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

This was a little more than a slow-burn- it was a bit of a forbidden romance, an enemies to lovers story, and a brother’s friend story. Yes.   <span id="freeText8627536024177657604" style="display:none"><b>4 stars!!!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%2010/19756501_10103972459156878_7667896498863354573_n_zpsspjfgg5j.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499679746i/23256891._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 19756501_10103972459156878_7667896498863354573_n_zpsspjfgg5j.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Under Locke</i> was another amazing read by the queen of slow-burn romance, Mariana Zapata. This was a little more than a slow-burn- it was a bit of a forbidden romance, an enemies to lovers story, and a brother’s friend story. Yes. A trifecta of awesomeness. <br><br>Iris Taylor’s life has been anything but easy. She’s had blow after blow since she was young, but that’s all in the past. She’s moving to Texas to start over. With the help of her older half brother, Sonny, she has a place to stay and a job to help get her back on her feet. The job is at a tattoo shop. That is where she meets Dex. Affectionately known as Dex the dick. Dex owns the shop, is friends with her brother, and a member of the MC her brother is a part of. And he’s a jerk to her at first. <br><br>  I was not a fan of Dex to start out with, but he slowly made me warm up to him, and by the end, I ended up loving him. Iris was a character with so much strength and perseverance. There were moments I wanted to holler at her for keeping things, but overall I liked her so much! She and Dex made sort of an odd couple, but I loved them together! <br><br><i>Under Locke</i> is not your typical MC book. It’s also a bit different than some of the other MZ books I have read. One of my favorite things about her writing is how she can make her books so different, yet the same in the way that makes me love them so much. As always, the audio book was fantastic. I flew through it looking for excuses to listen. I enjoyed this one lots! Recommended for all lovers of slow-burn romance. <br><i>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer831505378" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13365545809183249865">HOLY crap!! Am I really the first person to review this book???<br/><br/>Well.... In case you were wondering, I got my money's worth on this book!!! It was long, not too long, loved the characters.<br/><br/>Iris was recommended to be a tattoo artist front desk lady by her half brother Sonny. Sonny is friends with the owner(?) of the tattoo shop, Dex. Now they definitely don't have any immediate sexual tension. Dex was an ass to her. Both Iris and Dex are bad with new people. Iris because she's just super shy, and D</span>
  <span id="freeText13365545809183249865" style="display:none">HOLY crap!! Am I really the first person to review this book???<br /><br />Well.... In case you were wondering, I got my money's worth on this book!!! It was long, not too long, loved the characters.<br /><br />Iris was recommended to be a tattoo artist front desk lady by her half brother Sonny. Sonny is friends with the owner(?) of the tattoo shop, Dex. Now they definitely don't have any immediate sexual tension. Dex was an ass to her. Both Iris and Dex are bad with new people. Iris because she's just super shy, and Dex because he just doesn't like the process of people getting used to him, or that's what I gathered from his personality.<br /><br />Though Iris was really shy, and a beginning.. a pushover, she never did get on my nerves. Recently, I've been feeling real judgy towards heroines. I just find something that always bothers me. Thinking about it now, I don't think I was ever like that with Iris. <br />Even though she's mousy, she's still really strong. She finds the positive in really shitty situations. <br /><br />Dex is hawwtt! Sure in the beginning he was a dick to her, he had his reasons... not a reasonable reason, but a reason. I don't think he bothered me too.. GREAT CHARACTERS!!<br /><br />This couple does have a somewhat slow buildup. They don't get intimate until the last half of the book. I didn't really mind that because the author didn't bore with unnecessary details. For an MC book, this book doesn't have much angst, and again I'm totally ok with that.<br /><br />Overall, great read, worth my money, worth my time!!<br />Hopefully, you all enjoy this book as well as I did :D<br /><br /> </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2308763090" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2757428394739893719">Dex Locke:<b>
  <i> "You've gotta be the best thing I never knew I wanted."</i>
</b><br/>Iris Taylor: <b>
  <i>"I wanted to tell him that he was the best thing l never thought I'd have."</i>
</b><br/><br/>I met briefly Dex and Iris in Kulti's book. It was when Kulti went to Austin with Sal to have a tattoo and he had chosen the best shop, i.e. 'Pins and Needles'. <br/>I loved Sal's description of Dex:<br/><b>
  <i>"I'd never been a fan of guys that looked like they'd gone to jail, but you'd have to be blind to not appeciate how good-looking the man was,</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText2757428394739893719" style="display:none">Dex Locke:<b>
  <i> "You've gotta be the best thing I never knew I wanted."</i>
</b><br />Iris Taylor: <b>
  <i>"I wanted to tell him that he was the best thing l never thought I'd have."</i>
</b><br /><br />I met briefly Dex and Iris in Kulti's book. It was when Kulti went to Austin with Sal to have a tattoo and he had chosen the best shop, i.e. 'Pins and Needles'. <br />I loved Sal's description of Dex:<br /><b>
  <i>"I'd never been a fan of guys that looked like they'd gone to jail, but you'd have to be blind to not appeciate how good-looking the man was, even if he wasn't my type."</i>
</b><br />and<br /><b>
  <i>"My vagina didn't know what to do with itself."</i>
</b><br />And I loved Kulti's reaction:<br /><b>
  <i>"He's wearing a wedding ring."</i>
</b><br /><br />Well, I had to read "Under Locke" after that. It turned out to be another amazing story by Marianna Zapata!<br />A slow burn romance story of course. <br /><br />This time we have a biker with anger management issues (Dex) ... and a biker's daughter (Iris).<br />Iris knows nothing about Motorcycle clubs until she goes to stay with her half brother (Sonny) who is a member of the Widowmakers club, WMC.<br />Iris also does not know anything about piercings and tattoos until she starts working for Dex.<br />Finally Iris does not know much about sex until she starts sleeping with Dex.<br /><br />Iris and Dex did not like each other from the beginning. Dex saw Iris as an obligation. Iris saw Dex as a brute who made her angry and sad all the time and as a result she wanted to quit, but she needed the money. It is a kind of 'enemies to lovers' story, but the hatred will not last long because the book is really long and before it finishes you will probably have forgotten that they hated each other in the beginning.<br /><br />The book has its funny moments (Iris discovers the penis piercings), its painful moments (deaths, illnesses), its angst moments (Iris and Dex look for her douchebag father). <br />And of course my favourite grovelling moments (Dex has a lot to learn).<br /><br />• I believe if you like Motorcycle Club stories, you will like this book.<br />• Also, if you don't like Motorcycle Club stories, most probably you will like the book<br /><br />Win-win situation!</span>

<div id="review_852488272" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/852488272" />
    <a title="Sofia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17912911-sofia"><img alt="Sofia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438510615p2/17912911.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/852488272?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sofia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sofia" href="/user/show/17912911-sofia">Sofia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17912911-sofia?shelf=i-hate-you-but-i-love-you-romance">i-hate-you-but-i-love-you-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17912911-sofia?shelf=frustrating">frustrating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17912911-sofia?shelf=no-just-no">no-just-no</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17912911-sofia?shelf=can-t-take-seriously">can-t-take-seriously</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17912911-sofia?shelf=underdog-heroine">underdog-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17912911-sofia?shelf=annoying-heroine">annoying-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer852488272" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4929414655938450010">If you hate women you will absolutely love this book. <br/><br/>Well since I'm not masochistic it was a downright disgusting and painful read, but I really wanted to rate it so I barreled through. <br/><br/>Iris is the shy, insecure victim who, in her almost 25 years of life, have never had sex. <br/>Why? Why is it so important for the girl to always be a fucking virgin? I don't know why it's pissing me off except that it sends the wrong message to girls. That as soon as they have sex they're tainted and damaged goods o</span>
  <span id="freeText4929414655938450010" style="display:none">If you hate women you will absolutely love this book. <br /><br />Well since I'm not masochistic it was a downright disgusting and painful read, but I really wanted to rate it so I barreled through. <br /><br />Iris is the shy, insecure victim who, in her almost 25 years of life, have never had sex. <br />Why? Why is it so important for the girl to always be a fucking virgin? I don't know why it's pissing me off except that it sends the wrong message to girls. That as soon as they have sex they're tainted and damaged goods or something. Womens worth is somehow wrapped up in how many sexual partners they've had.<br />And Dex, obviously he is a moody, possessive horndog. And since he is a guy the same rules does not apply to him. I just kept waiting for Iris to snap and tell him to fuck off. He gets to have casual sex with whoever but she's not even allowed to talk to guys? She's a fragile flower that can't go to the store without an escort and can't under any circumstances live alone. She's not allowed to make her own goddamn decisions about <u>anything</u>. <br /><br />Iris, like many main female characters, have beer flavored nipples. She cannot leave her home without guys assaulting her left, right and center. And I hate how those moments (they're many btw) feel so incredibly choreographed, because it's only so Dex can show up and get in the guy's face and save the day.<br />When Dex told her to button up her cardigan because she was showing a little to much collarbone(?), I wanted to reach into the book a slap him silly. Iris already dress like a sixty year old librarian. Why not just demand that she wear a burka?<br /><br />It's also one of those books where she hates him, he acts like an asshole, sexual tension and then floodgates of mushy love.<br /> <br />I guess it had a little potential. And had it been less cliché and Iris had been given a backbone, then maybe I would have enjoyed it. Maybe.<br /><br />Oh, and I hate how much Iris felt sorry for herself. It made me feel less sorry for her because of it. Having gone through everything that she had, I would think she'd have a little tougher skin. But if someone so much as looked at her funny her lip started quivering. It just didn't feel believable that she could be that meek with that upbringing. I mean, I'm not even that meek and life hasn't handed me that many lemons.<br /><br />And this was sadly just the tip of the iceberg. So anyway, rant over.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4929414655938450010" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer831436015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4962687100302919938">I loved this. <br/><br/>Admittedly, it took me a couple of chapters to get into it, at first the writing seems a bit choppy and a cpl of times I had to go back a page or two to remind myself of a question a character had asked.<br/><br/>However, once it settles and who was who, what connected them and the history of the characters made itself known, it just flowed and I started to really enjoy it.<br/><br/>Iris Taylor has had a hard life. She has had to move across country and move in with her half brother who is part of the</span>
  <span id="freeText4962687100302919938" style="display:none">I loved this. <br /><br />Admittedly, it took me a couple of chapters to get into it, at first the writing seems a bit choppy and a cpl of times I had to go back a page or two to remind myself of a question a character had asked.<br /><br />However, once it settles and who was who, what connected them and the history of the characters made itself known, it just flowed and I started to really enjoy it.<br /><br />Iris Taylor has had a hard life. She has had to move across country and move in with her half brother who is part of the MC club their father used to be part of. Sonny gets her a job with a fellow Widow MC member at his tattoo shop.<br /><br />Charles Dexter Locke (aka Charlie or The Dick) does not get off to the best start with Iris "Ritz".<br /><br />On her second day in the job she hears him insulting her. And boy can this girl hold a grudge. It went on for a few weeks, but she is fully aware of how unreasonable it is in all honesty, she just cant help herself!<br /><br /><i>
  <b> I was surprised by how nice everyone had been-with the exception of Dex's dumb face.<br />....<br />All of this assured me that I'd avoided having to interact much with my boss. The owner. The bleeding mouth sore.<br /><br />The snot-faced ass hole that I only kind-of, sort-of hoped came down with an infectious illness in his private parts. But you know, something he could get medicine for.<br /><br />....<br /><br />Dex was a temperamental bag of beaver dung.<br /></b>
</i><br /><br />ooh, and my favourite, which I think will become my insult of choice for the next few months <i>
  <b> Duke Dickface</b>
</i><br /><br />But it has been said there is a fine line between love and hate.<br /><br />Iris, at first she took Dex's crap, while insulting him in her mind and giving knee capping rights to her brother, but soon she starts to stand up for herself and is not going to take his crap any more.<br /><br />Over the next few weeks they slowly start to get to know each other, slowly becoming friends and then more. It was lovely to watch their relationship change and grow from where it first started. <br /><br />There was no real angst in their relationship once it had grown to a point of being more than friends....any conflict was from outside their relationship...mainly Iris's deadbeat dad and his issues causing them trouble. <br /><br />It is rare I like the heroine as much as the hero in a book, but I really liked Iris, with her insults and "That's what she said" jokes and high fives. There was just something very endearing about her.<br /><br />And Dex, yes he was a dick at first, but as we get to know him better and how he interacts and deals with Iris, you could not help but fall in love with him too <i>
  <b> The Kindest, grumpy ass man in all of Texas</b>
</i><br /><br />All in all, it was a hugely enjoyable read, and the slow build up of the relationship between Dex and Iris was beautiful to experience. <br /><br /><b>
  <i> "you've gotta be the best thing I never knew I wanted"<br /><br />.........<br /><br />"Seen a lot of things in my life - But you" His nostrils flared "my sweet, sweet baby, have gotta be my favourite by far"</i>
</b><br /><br />An excellent 5 star read for me. <br /><br />I would love to read about Sonny, Tripp, the guys from the tattoo parlour and even Luther!<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4962687100302919938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2828810769" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11158808507277927632">22/03/2020<br/><br/>Just re-read this because M. Zapata has it as a freebie on Amazon (in case anyone is interested) and I had it on KU last time. <br/><br/>Anyway, it was as good as I remembered. I’ve noticed things that escaped me before - or rather, I didn’t appreciate as much before. I was saying a million Hell Yes’es in my head while Iris was giving Dex some lessons in human interaction 101 lol. <br/><br/>But honestly, I totally loved Iris. She had loads of self respect. Was she insecure and naive at times? Sure. But at</span>
  <span id="freeText11158808507277927632" style="display:none">22/03/2020<br /><br />Just re-read this because M. Zapata has it as a freebie on Amazon (in case anyone is interested) and I had it on KU last time. <br /><br />Anyway, it was as good as I remembered. I’ve noticed things that escaped me before - or rather, I didn’t appreciate as much before. I was saying a million Hell Yes’es in my head while Iris was giving Dex some lessons in human interaction 101 lol. <br /><br />But honestly, I totally loved Iris. She had loads of self respect. Was she insecure and naive at times? Sure. But at the core she was strong. Despite saying how hot Dex was about 10000x times she didn’t once act like she lost her brain cells because of it. <br /><br />Dex was ... Dex. I mean I did like the guy. He gave me some really alpha male vibes, I’d just rather praise Iris cause she was the more interesting character for once. Sure, he had layers too, but this is one of those very few times in a romance book that I loved how the heroine acted, talked and held her own. (She did some pretty stupid shit at some point but I mean we all have our tstl moments - and it was just a moment, not a pattern of behaviour lol) <br /><br />Also, I wanna mention that this might be the only book where I really don’t mind the 24 yr heroine being a virgin. I mean, I kinda get how that would happen in her situation. Could I do without that tidbit and the double standard it usually enforces? Sure. Was it perpetuating a trend where the heroines need to be pure to be more worthy? NO. It really did make sense for her and her individual situation. <br /><br />Long story short... I need another Zapata slow burn and I think the time has come for From Lukov with Love.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11158808507277927632" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1073490970682027074"><b>5/5 stars</b><br/><br/><b>reread:</b> <br/>02/07/17<br/>10/10/17<br/>17/03/18<br/>24/06/18<br/>23/11/18<br/>18/05/19<br/>25/03/20<br/><br/><s>this is beginning to get ridiculous, but I still adore this book every time I read it, it's my comfort read</s><br/><br/>SO I reread this only a week after finishing it, I just couldn't get the characters out of my head and I didn't want to read anything but this. And I don't regret a thing. I loved it just as much the second time around, I relate hardcore to Iris and I just want a Dex for myself. I highlighted some of my favourite passa</span>
  <span id="freeText1073490970682027074" style="display:none"><b>5/5 stars</b><br><br><b>reread:</b> <br>02/07/17<br>10/10/17<br>17/03/18<br>24/06/18<br>23/11/18<br>18/05/19<br>25/03/20<br><br><s>this is beginning to get ridiculous, but I still adore this book every time I read it, it's my comfort read</s><br><br>SO I reread this only a week after finishing it, I just couldn't get the characters out of my head and I didn't want to read anything but this. And I don't regret a thing. I loved it just as much the second time around, I relate hardcore to Iris and I just want a Dex for myself. I highlighted some of my favourite passages this time around so I'm just going to add them into the review.<br><br>HOLY HELL. I loved this book more than I can say, I was up <i>wayy</i> too late finishing this and I could not put it down. Dex was the ultimate male—protective, tattooed, accomplished and so, so attractive. <br><br><b>AND HE IS A TATTOO ARTIST?!</b> um hell yes, please &amp; thank you.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497791463ra/23057602.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book follows Iris as she moves in with her half-brother Sonny, a member of the Widow MC. Iris takes a job as a receptionist at Dex's tattoo parlor, another fellow Widow biker who immediately does not like the look of Iris. The two immediately butt heads, they banter and they bicker and I loved it. <br><br>Slowly they're brought together when rival gangs come looking for the money that Iris and Sonny's father owed them, making the siblings collateral damage. <br><br>I adored Iris, I loved every awkward moment and dialog and I couldn't get enough of her. Iris was a character who had battled through an extremely tough life, losing her mother and grandmother, leaving her to finish raising her brother while battling health issues. I originally found her character to be a little meek, but when her background was discovered, it gave me a new appreciation for her character.<br><br>I don't think every female character has to be tough as nails on the outside to be admired. She was resilient and bounced back no matter what life threw at her, sometimes they're the people that win the most respect from me. I related to her so much, I'm a person who wears their heart on their sleeve. <br><br><blockquote>"Then again, I always wanted to cry. I cried when I was happy, sad, excited and frustrated with life. And I hated it. Especially now."</blockquote><br><br>This book was fun, angsty and adorable, I loved every moment and it ended way too quickly. This had a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> vibe to it, probably reminding me most of her book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18679675.Sweet_Dreams__Colorado_Mountain___2_" title="Sweet Dreams (Colorado Mountain, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Dreams</a>. The relationship between the characters and the build-up is extremely similar!<br><br>And just try and say no to this man. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497791463ra/23057603.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dex is a man who loves Firefly. Um, I couldn't ask for anything more. <br><br><blockquote>"You like Firefly. That's pretty nerdy."</blockquote> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498201432ra/23104336.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7218093944991967943">I know Zapata books are famous for the slow-burn romances. I loved her other book <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24044596.Kulti' title='Kulti by Mariana Zapata' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kulti</a> which made me decide to read some of her other books. <br/>Dex and Iris make a guest appearance in Kulti which made me select this as my next read as I really wanted to know more about them.<br/><br/>Even before I started with this one, I knew looking at some of the reviews this is not as good as Kulti and my verdict is the same. It is nowhere near as good as Kulti. It maybe unfair to compare it to another book even though </span>
  <span id="freeText7218093944991967943" style="display:none">I know Zapata books are famous for the slow-burn romances. I loved her other book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24044596.Kulti" title="Kulti by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">Kulti</a> which made me decide to read some of her other books. <br>Dex and Iris make a guest appearance in Kulti which made me select this as my next read as I really wanted to know more about them.<br><br>Even before I started with this one, I knew looking at some of the reviews this is not as good as Kulti and my verdict is the same. It is nowhere near as good as Kulti. It maybe unfair to compare it to another book even though they are by the same author but somehow as a reader, after reading Kulti certain expectations and standards were set.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493731441ra/22646570.gif" height="" width="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Iris starts working in an Tattoo parlor under duress and her boss is Dex Locke. Iris and Dex start their work relation on the wrong footing:<br><b>
  <i>"So in my head it made sense that my work day had been spent A)ignoring Dex, B)avoiding Dex, and C)getting to know my coworkers slowly."</i>
</b><br><br><b>Now after knowing the name of the main characters the title does sound a bit cheesy.</b><br><br>I liked that there was more to it than just the romance <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The cancer fight that Iris has to go through and in her way she has emerged strong from it. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. The character of Iris is what made me continue with this story.<br><br>The romance aspect of it moved very slowly but it works well with the story. <b>It is a very laid-back story without any angst.</b> <br><br>I am not a fan of Biker Romances and this is what it is. That part of it somehow did not click with me. <br>Somethings were left unresolved even in the epilogue and I really want to know what happened <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[with Will. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Overall a very average one time read and hence the 2 stars.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText11799680943432378548" style="display:none"><b>★4.5★</b><blockquote>
  <b>"You’ve gotta be the best thing I never knew I wanted."</b>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1552790512i/27216655._SX540_.png" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Under Locke</b> is another brilliant slow burn romance by the "Slow Burn Queen" Mariana Zapata! With forbidden romance, motorcycles, a smoking hot tatted bad boy, and one spunky heroine, <b>Under Locke</b> is 497 pages of pure goodness. Iris Taylor just moved to Austin and lands a job working as a receptionist at a tattoo shop. Her boss Dex is everything Iris is NOT! He is cocky, gruff, and confident. Although Iris is determined to embrace this amazing opportunity for a fresh start, she cannot help but be completely smitten with her bad boy boss. When Iris finds herself in a world of trouble, Dex is quick to offer Iris his protection, friendship, and love! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448780071i/17188579.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>"The urge to fall to the ground, rip my heart out of my chest and hold it out like a sacred offering was overwhelming."</b>
</blockquote> <b>Under Locke</b> is another complex story with lyrical writing, action, and slow burn romance at its finest! Iris and Dex are complete opposites and yet together they make a perfect match. Although both main characters carry a great deal of baggage, together they are able to overcome so much! As always, Ms. Zapata's writing is fluid and beautifully constructed with a cast of unforgettable characters, passion, and beautiful romance!<blockquote>
  <b>"Baby, just ‘cuz you’re cute doesn’t mean I wasn’t bein’ serious about spankin’ your tight little ass for doin’ dumb shit, Ritz. You do it again, and you’re gonna get it."</b>
</blockquote> Overall, <b>Under Locke</b> would appeal to MC Romance fans or slow burn romance lovers! I highly recommend any and all of Mariana Zapata's work. <div id="review_1292334237" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1292334237" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1292334237?book_show_action=true">May 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=unable-to-put-down">unable-to-put-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=angst-in-my-pants">angst-in-my-pants</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=hot-as-hell">hot-as-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=betrayal">betrayal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=workplace-affair">workplace-affair</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1292334237" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16264358910786232814">4.5 STARS<br/><br/>Ever since reading the book that literally put me in the worst book slump ever, because it was so effing fantastic, I've made it my mission to read everything MZ has or will ever write. That book is Kulti. I still get goose bumps when I see it. It might seem irrational? Maybe others who've read it are scratching their heads, but to me, it was the gold standard. <br/>Anyways...this was really, really good. I loved it. I'm also glad I waited so long after finishing Kulti, because anything woul</span>
  <span id="freeText16264358910786232814" style="display:none">4.5 STARS<br /><br />Ever since reading the book that literally put me in the worst book slump ever, because it was so effing fantastic, I've made it my mission to read everything MZ has or will ever write. That book is Kulti. I still get goose bumps when I see it. It might seem irrational? Maybe others who've read it are scratching their heads, but to me, it was the gold standard. <br />Anyways...this was really, really good. I loved it. I'm also glad I waited so long after finishing Kulti, because anything would have paled compared to that and I wanted my mind open and not hung up on how good this author's previous book was. I've seen this being compared to Kristen Ashley's work...hmmm...yes. I see that. BUT. But it wasn't like it either, from what I've read by her, anyway.<br />KA seems to have cornered the market on rough and tough alphas that don't say a lot but are sexy and dominant as sin. Since I've read those types of characterizations before, I just wanted to emphasize that they've been around a long time, just written with a different spin. Take Christian Grey, for example. And a plethora of others, they all fit that characterization so why does one author seem to only get the credit? What I'm trying to say is I didn't think Dex Locke was classic KA. Besides, I really liked Iris, the heroine, and at least I saw why she was special, unlike some of KA's heroines. I'm not dissing, just pointing out some differences. <br /><br />I usually don't like MC books, but again, this author can probably make me like anything I've sworn off. There was an urgency in finishing this. The pacing was fantastic, I was never bored and this baby was long. There was also a nice, slow burn...I adore those. I loved Dex, but hated him at first. He was so mean sometimes! But as he got to see Iris for who she was and not what he thought, things changed drastically. Dex was sexy and sweet, aggressive yet tender. Iris was a great girl. Having gone through so much I was glad she ended up with a man like Dex. This was also very hot. Never overdone, but extremely sexy. I remember towards the end of Kulti there was a scene where Kulti and Sal head to a tattoo place run by a Dex Locke. They meet a woman named Iris, too. It's funny that I later read that those characters were from MZ's previous book, then when I finally read this I felt like racing back and re-reading that scene in Kulti with them. Both books are standalones though, and completely unrelated, so no worries. <br />Anyways, loved this!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16264358910786232814" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=books-2020">books-2020</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/104884953-apoorva?shelf=antiheroes-bad-boys">antiheroes-bad-boys</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3402884031" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer835831503007187314"><i>Edit: Re-read a few good parts because this is one of Zapata's books that I have selective memory for🙈 (yes that implies that I am BIASED).</i><br/><br/>Okay so I'm gonna go ahead and say this- I totally had a love-hate relationship with this one for like 60-70%. One minute I liked them and the next I was shaking my head so hard, my neck was aching.<br/><br/>This review isn't going to be coherent at all, and as it is there are a lot of amazing ones. <br/>Did I like this? Duh. Of course yes! It's Mariana Zapata and it's hard</span>
  <span id="freeText835831503007187314" style="display:none"><i>Edit: Re-read a few good parts because this is one of Zapata's books that I have selective memory for🙈 (yes that implies that I am BIASED).</i><br /><br />Okay so I'm gonna go ahead and say this- I totally had a love-hate relationship with this one for like 60-70%. One minute I liked them and the next I was shaking my head so hard, my neck was aching.<br /><br />This review isn't going to be coherent at all, and as it is there are a lot of amazing ones. <br />Did I like this? Duh. Of course yes! It's Mariana Zapata and it's hard to not like anything by her. (Yeah, I am biased)<br />I felt more connected to Iris in this one as opposed to both characters, like in Zapata's other books. Don't misunderstand- I liked Dex <i>a hell lot</i> but just not as much as I liked Iris in this one. She was a little naive, but also innocent, loyal and I could see that she had toughened up by the end. I loved her <i>'that's what she said'</i> moments. I also liked how she went from woe-is-me to badass chick the next moment. She didn't let bad things hold her down or wallow in self pity for too long.<br /><br />Dex, my man- it was difficult not to like him by the end. At almost 50% I was oscillating between "What the hell, man?" and "Aw he's so good". He was short tempered (ha), possessive, so.....alpha-like (but not in the typical way of MC Bikers bitch, more like protective), and fiercely loyal. That was one thing that I felt was the most common between the two- they were <i>really</i> loyal. And it doesn't bother that he was hot. Iris was all swoony after him since the start, but not when he was actually talking to her, so it was nice to see that she didn't let the lower half of her body control the upper half. But I get that girl- if it were me, I would be swooning too- but only from a distance. God knows bikers aren't for me. 😂<br /><br />I abso-friggin-lutely loved Sonny and Slim! Sonny was an amazing brother- protective, not too overbearing but not entirely laid back either. I would go as far to say that he was a little more (don't shoot) protective and loving than Dex. And yes Ms Zapata, this is my way of <s>demanding</s> politely requesting another book from you. Slim was a terrific friend too, he would win all the brownie points if I ever gave even one. <br /><br />So there, this thing is just for the record- to entice me to read it again and remind me how much I wanted to punch and then hug Iris and Dex. And I'm probably reminiscing the time when they made an appearance in Kulti *sigh*.</span>
  <a data-text-id="835831503007187314" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2023808882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7907621210529770907"><b>4 stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511975792ra/24561132.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>I’d never been a big fan of that saying, “Everything happens for a reason,” but maybe, sometimes, every once in a while, things coalesced into a complex, intangible reason. With tattoos and piercings and bad words and unfailing loyalty topped with a temper. And in its own imperfect way, it couldn’t have been any better.</i>
</b><i></i><br/><br/>Iris Taylor is starting over in a new town. She left behind haunting memories and heartaches back in Florida. Her biker half-brother, Sonny, is helping her get back on</span>
  <span id="freeText7907621210529770907" style="display:none"><b>4 stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511975792ra/24561132.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I’d never been a big fan of that saying, “Everything happens for a reason,” but maybe, sometimes, every once in a while, things coalesced into a complex, intangible reason. With tattoos and piercings and bad words and unfailing loyalty topped with a temper. And in its own imperfect way, it couldn’t have been any better.</i>
</b><i></i><br><br>Iris Taylor is starting over in a new town. She left behind haunting memories and heartaches back in Florida. Her biker half-brother, Sonny, is helping her get back on her feet. She is crashing with him until she makes enough money to find her own place. He scored her a job at a local tattoo shop; the owner is Son’s friend and part of the same MC club. Iris is nervous about working in a tattoo shop as that isn’t really her <i>scene.</i> Now, however, she is determined to find employment elsewhere because the owner, Dex the Dick, is just that – a dick.<br><br>And Dex knows he is a hard-ass. He has his own issues and takes his anger out on the undeserving. He believes that Iris is just going to have to adjust to his crabby attitude. Because she isn't going anywhere.<br><br><b>
  <i>Babe, I've handpicked everythin' and everyone in here. I know what I want and I get what I want," he breathed. "And I keep what's mine.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451863456ra/17614620.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>MZ is amazingly talented. She can bring a story to life like no other. <i>Under Locke</i> was not my favorite of her books, but it was still <b>really</b> good. It was actually refreshing to see a biker romance not be so dark and edgy. Of course, leave MZ to be the one to pull that off. <i>Did I mention how talented she is?</i> I only have one more book by her to read, and it saddens me. However, I did some <s>stalking</s> researching and found that she is hoping to release another book in February 2018. <br><br>Although I am only giving this book 4 stars, I still <u>highly</u> recommend it. If you are a fan of slow-burn tales, alpha men, and personable characters – this one is for you. Honestly, just read all of her books. They are amazing!<br><br></span>

  <span id="freeText3627048681223636820" style="display:none"><i>Review written May 9, 2016</i><br><br><b>3.8 Stars - Nice and fun, a tiny bit too 'longish', but all in all very good</b><br><br>Yes it is strange but true, I went from listening to one MC Club m/f (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/508075270?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Chaos #1</a> by KA) directly to another one. Even, yes even, if I'm not even sure I like (or can fully tolerate) these <i>MC club world</i>'s in my romances. Well, we don't always do what best for us. Or? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389119833ra/7991749.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> • <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389119833ra/7991749.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> • <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389119833ra/7991749.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> • <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389119833ra/7991749.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This time was it a pretty sweet and nice MC story by an author that already impressed me with her wonderful funny and lighthearted female football (soccer) romance <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1571000828?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Kulti</a> (4.7 stars) some months ago. This one, <i>Under Locke</i> wasn't in the same amazing great class but without doubt good enough. My like!!<br><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>Iris Taylor</b> isn't the worlds most lucky or fortunated girl. When her bank account is more and less empty, after six months as unemployed, she has to take her car and drive the long way from home in <i>Florida</i> to stay with her older half brother <i>Sonny</i> in <i>Austin, Texas</i>. <br><br>Her brother is a member in the local MC club, he is a tough <i>
  <u>Widower</u>
</i>. The same club her since long dissapered looser dad was a brother in and so is also her pretty scary new boss ... the sexy drool worthy <b>Dex Locke</b>.<br><blockquote>
  <i>« ~ it was either the strip club or the tattoo shop. <br>... she should have chosen the strip club. »</i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Bodypart/image_zpswxvgvrpq.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446394459i/16801308.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpswxvgvrpq.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><b>Once again hooked — Ms. Zapata know how to do it...</b><br>This one had a lot. A very funny narration by a great heroine in poor Iris. A heroine I also truly admired and liked. Add a swoon worthy tough sexy alpha biker hero and bunch of lovely (easy to like) second characters. — <i>Under Locke</i> was another romantic, mostly lighthearted and truly enjoying story by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5760202.Mariana_Zapata" title="Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">Mariana Zapata</a>. Her stories are kind of slow developed and you need to be a bit patient if you want steamy scenes. Best of all, her style is entertaining amusing witty with admirable innocent (on the smex history but not about life) wisely sweet heroines. From now on is this lady on my "authors to read / listening to everything by" list. (Next up should hopefully soon be <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30120594.The_Wall_of_Winnipeg_and_Me" title="The Wall of Winnipeg and Me by Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">The Wall of Winnipeg and Me</a>.)<br><br><b>This audiobook edition, the narrator...</b><br>I listened to the 16 hours audiobook narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7438028.Callie_Dalton" title="Callie Dalton" rel="nofollow noopener">Callie Dalton</a>, a narrator doing her job in a style I very much like. Will be more romances narrated by her.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>I LIKE - to not like "bikers", wrinkle my nose and read anyway..</b><br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="3627048681223636820" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14280747168174794500">5 stars for the Queen of slow-burn romance.<br/>I picked this book up without reading the blurb as I am so smitten with this author's writing and ability to tell a story that I had no doubt I would enjoy it and I really did. In fact I ended up loving this book.<br/>I admire the way Mariana slowly builds up the story and develops her characters, making them deep, complex and very real. <br/>Take this book for instance. I was fairly certain along with Iris (our heroine) that Dex was an absolute "dick" and I wasn</span>
  <span id="freeText14280747168174794500" style="display:none">5 stars for the Queen of slow-burn romance.<br />I picked this book up without reading the blurb as I am so smitten with this author's writing and ability to tell a story that I had no doubt I would enjoy it and I really did. In fact I ended up loving this book.<br />I admire the way Mariana slowly builds up the story and develops her characters, making them deep, complex and very real. <br />Take this book for instance. I was fairly certain along with Iris (our heroine) that Dex was an absolute "dick" and I wasn't sure how he was ever going to redeem himself in my eyes but as this story unfolded I really came to like and respect him. He was always smoking hot though!<br />I think that is Mariana's secret weapon she gives us these unlikely heroes that we eventually end up falling hard for.<br />The slow buildup is definitely worth it and the last 25-30% of this book was so satisfying and sexy.<br />Great read.</span>

<div id="review_2119305099" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2119305099" />
    <a title="Kaila" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35924884-kaila"><img alt="Kaila" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1533304308p2/35924884.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2119305099?book_show_action=true">Sep 11, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kaila" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kaila" href="/user/show/35924884-kaila">Kaila</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=swoon-worthy-love-interest">swoon-worthy-love-interest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=heart-warming-stories">heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=slow-burn">slow-burn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35924884-kaila?shelf=hate-to-love">hate-to-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2119305099" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1024770646686527285"><b>3.5/5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“You’ve gotta be the best thing I never knew I wanted.” </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>I just flew through this story!! </b>I've been fully captivated by this slow-burning romance novel for the last few days, and now all I want to do is binge this author's other books. Dex and Iris had an emotional journey full of humour, romance and friendship. I absolutely loved the slow pace to their romance as I could become full enveloped in their story and watching their relationship grow an thrive. <i>Under Locke</i> was a <b>beautifu</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1024770646686527285" style="display:none"><b>3.5/5 stars</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“You’ve gotta be the best thing I never knew I wanted.” </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>I just flew through this story!! </b>I've been fully captivated by this slow-burning romance novel for the last few days, and now all I want to do is binge this author's other books. Dex and Iris had an emotional journey full of humour, romance and friendship. I absolutely loved the slow pace to their romance as I could become full enveloped in their story and watching their relationship grow an thrive. <i>Under Locke</i> was a <b>beautifully heartwarming</b> story that has left me feeling so happy inside. This is my first book by this author, but I already feel like I've <b>fallen in love</b> with her writing style.<br /><br />Iris Taylor has movies to Austen to live with her half brother after a difficult time in her already tough life. She has found herself unemployed, but her half brother has given her an opportunity to work at a tattoo parlour. The one'll problem is, Iris is nothing like these people. She wears cardigans, doesn't drink much and tends to stay in rather than go out partying. Iris' half brother and his friends are Widowers, a MC club that her estranged father was also apart of. Iris has to try and fit in with her new world whilst trying to deal with her boss, Dex Locke, who seems to hate her.<br /><br />Dex Locke is an ex-felon who is both dangerously good looking as well as being immensely intimidating. Despite this, Iris refuses to be bullied by him and his harsh regime. She can't afford to lose this job, so Iris tries her hardest to stand up for herself. Through doing this, she forms an unlikely friendship with Dex that seems laced with an underlying sexual tension. As his fondness for her grows into something romantic , Iris must decide whether she feels safe opening herself up to someone, especially after a life of heartache and loss.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>“Babe, I've handpicked everythin' and everyone in here. I know what I want and I get what I want," he breathed. "And I keep what's mine.” </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>I fell into this book completely </b>and was fully enveloped in the story. There were so many interesting aspects that were subtle and interesting. I'd hadn't even realise how much I had read until I looked at the page numbers and saw that I was almost finished when I had only started it a couple of hours earlier. I didn't think about anything else but this book while I was reading it, <b>my whole life seemed to fade away while I was holding the pages</b>, that's how engaging this book is. The friendships that Iris made at the shop, the small stories from her past, the relationship with Dex and just her overall emotional journey all tied the story together. It was well rounded, believable, authentic and just <b>completely engaging.</b><br /><br />The romance in this book was just really <b>heartwarming</b>. It was definitely more of a slow burn, but it was still as intense as I had hoped for. It was as if I was reading a friendship story with chemistry and before I knew it I was rooting for these two characters. They had a bit of a rocky start, but it just added to the humour of the story. I wouldn't say that it was a hate-to-love relationship, but more of a banter-to-love situation. I did love these characters together,e but I felt like their plot was getting a bit repetitive at times. Despite this, the romance was still my favourite element of the book.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1024770646686527285" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14118955992731746504" style="display:none">I'm late on posting a rating for this book. My family got sick and then passed it to me. Once I was recovered my laptop cord broke. When it rains it pours. So, I'm behind in reviews and blogging. <br><br>Since it's been awhile since I listened to it... I'll make this quick. The cover has a motorcycle on it and while this has some elements of a<i> motorcycle romance </i> I wouldn't categorise it a hardcore <u>Sons of Anarchy</u> type of book. If you like slow to burn romance then give this one a try. I enjoyed listening to it. ♥<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459059798i/18564417._SX540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>STANDALONE</b><br><br>I won this book and 2 others (Kulti &amp; The Wall of Winnipeg &amp; Me) from Book Babes Unite giveaway. <div id="review_838707882" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/838707882" />
    <a title="Michelle [Helen Geek]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5557851-michelle-helen-geek"><img alt="Michelle [Helen Geek]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448463806p2/5557851.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/838707882?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle [Helen Geek]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle [Helen Geek]" href="/user/show/5557851-michelle-helen-geek">Michelle [Helen Geek]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone. A nice solid read</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Michelle by: </span>
      GR KA Ladies
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=tbr-kindle">tbr-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=author_love">author_love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=challenge-books-read-2014">challenge-books-read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=keep-to-read-again">keep-to-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=were-pub-d-in-2014-i-read">were-pub-d-in-2014-i-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=stands-alone">stands-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=gr-high-recommend">gr-high-recommend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5557851-michelle-helen-geek?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer838707882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12542116743349223916">03/10/2016 -- Re-read this and enjoyed it as much the second time. Maybe a bit more.<br/><br/>02/02/2014 -- Original read<br/><b><br/>Overall Rating = 4 Stars<br/>Book Cover / Book Blurb / Book Title = 3 / 3 / 4 = 3.5 Stars<br/>Writer’s Voice = 4 Stars<br/>Character Development = 4 Stars<br/>Story Appreciation = 4 Stars<br/>Worth the Chili = 5 Stars -- [$2.99 on Amazon]<br/>Smexy [HEAT] Rating = Mild<br/>915 pages, but felt more like 450 or so.<br/></b><br/>I really enjoyed this one. I've seen it compared to Kristen Ashley, maybe. If so, it was much better. As much </span>
  <span id="freeText12542116743349223916" style="display:none">03/10/2016 -- Re-read this and enjoyed it as much the second time. Maybe a bit more.<br /><br />02/02/2014 -- Original read<br /><b><br />Overall Rating = 4 Stars<br />Book Cover / Book Blurb / Book Title = 3 / 3 / 4 = 3.5 Stars<br />Writer’s Voice = 4 Stars<br />Character Development = 4 Stars<br />Story Appreciation = 4 Stars<br />Worth the Chili = 5 Stars -- [$2.99 on Amazon]<br />Smexy [HEAT] Rating = Mild<br />915 pages, but felt more like 450 or so.<br /></b><br />I really enjoyed this one. I've seen it compared to Kristen Ashley, maybe. If so, it was much better. As much as I loved Sweet Dreams, there were places in it that didn't sit well with me and I thought was clunky. I gave it 5 Stars because it was unique, at the time.<br /><br />I think Mariana Zapata has skill. I think her prose flow smoothly and it appears like she does her research. Something I've found sadly lacking with KA; especially after the new wore off for me. You plan and do your research you are light years above those who don't and just need to wait for that break through opportunity. I think this is it for Ms. Zapata.<br /><br />Note: I have seen this commented on as being MC light. Not sure what they mean by this other than to say, it doesn't have all the violent triggers you have in some other books. I don't consider that a bad thing. I can read it with or without. What I can't abide is a terrible story. So, MC light or not, is it good? This one is definitely good.<br /><br /><b>So, what stood out for me on this one?</b><br />1 -- The characters. It seems to always come to the characters for me. Loved Sonnie. Dex was perfection and Iris? I haven't loved a heroine so much in quite some time. I loved how she powered through her fears and found that inner courage. I loved how she didn't want anyone to feel sorry for her. I loved how she loved and cared for those around her. This girl had taken some knocks and was the very definition of the phrase, "what doesn't kill you makes you stronger."<br /><br />2 -- The storytelling ability of this author is really good. Not perfect or even terribly unique, but good. She builds relationships slowly, but never bores the reader. She creates these really tough, but likeable characters. You don't have this immediate like, but rather a slow building respect for them. No insta-love here. Perfect really.<br /><br />3 -- The title for this book. I really liked it. I wondered about it before I bought it. Now, I think it was selected with care and is really appropriate for the book.<br /><br />4 -- The intimacy between Ritz and Dex is really nice. These two like each other and care about each other and you get that their attraction is much more than sex.<br /><br />5 -- The length of the book was really nice. LOVE a nice, long, sink your teeth into it, read.<br /><br />6 -- I don't think this is part of a series, but if it is, it stands alone and has no cliffhanger. Gotta love it!!<br /><br /><b>Now, for a few things that fell short for me.</b><br />1 - The story wasn't unique. I saw a bit of Sweet Dreams when I compare Tate and Dex. However, I think I liked Dex a bit better. He was more believable for me. He wasn't painted as this perfect alpha. He had a tender, more caring side to him and spoke in multiple syllables. That whole "Me Tarzen, You Jane" thing with Tate got on my nerves after a while. I actually think I liked this story better. I liked these characters better, but, now, because I've read Sweet Dreams, I can see some comparison. Ms. Zapata has made this her own, but, you can see where she may have gotten some of her idea.<br /><br />2 -- I absolutely hate the 24 year old virgin thing. HATE it. This one wasn't as annoying as some, but it still bothered me. I don't believe it and even more importantly, why do I care and why do I want to read about it? I don't. Saying this, if you are like me, I'd tell you to read this. I don't think you will be disappointed, just maybe a bit perterbed ;)<br /><br />3 -- I thought the ending a bit rushed and lacked a bit of clarification and grace. We spent so much time in the book looking for the dad. Searching, searching, searching ... Then, we have a brief encounter and the book ends about 20 or so pages later. I hate when an author feels like they need to "wrap up" the story and it happens with so little grace. I wasn't left hanging, but felt the ending clunky and lacked the polish of much of the rest of the book.<br /><br />I will definitely read more by this author. She does a very nice job. I found this on a thread I follow on GR's and want to thank those ladies for paving the way and telling us how good this one is. They were very right on this one!<br /><br />Happy Reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12542116743349223916" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
